Six Organizations Actively Building a Giant Bell for Jiuhua Mountain 160

Weighing 18,000 Catties. Audible Ten Li Away.

The six organizations that initiated the project to build the Youming Giant Bell for Jiuhua Mountain in Anhui—the Chinese Buddhist Association, the Shanghai Buddhist Association, the Jiuhua Buddhist Association, the Buddhist Pure Land Society, the World Buddhist Laymen's Association, and the Buddhist Bookstore—have seen enthusiastic donations pouring in from all sides. The giant bell will be made entirely of bronze and weigh 18,000 catties. The entire Ksitigarbha Sutra will be engraved on the bell. A bell tower will be built at the summit of Jiuhua Mountain, with one story dedicated to hanging the giant bell and housing a statue of Ksitigarbha Bodhisattva. The lower story will house people. The fundraising target is 48,000 yuan, divided into 24,000 shares, with each share costing two yuan. The names of all donors will be engraved on the four walls of the bell tower as a memorial. Sufficient funds have already been raised, and construction will begin soon. The project is expected to take two years to complete. Once the bell is finished, it will be audible ten li away each time it is rung. The six organizations plan to invite Buddhist figures from all over to participate in a grand prayer ceremony at Jiuhua Mountain upon the completion of the giant bell.

Tang Hai'an, Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Rowe, Customs Commissioner, jointly issued Proclamation No. 1443 yesterday, stating that they had received an order from the Ministry of Finance issuing regulations on the control of sodium oxide (i.e., sodium chloride), instructing them to comply immediately. Therefore, compliance is required. Hereafter, all sodium oxide imported or transshipped must be accompanied by a sodium chloride license issued by the Ministry of Finance for tax collection and release. In addition to posting the aforementioned regulations in the General Affairs Section of this Customs House to ensure public knowledge, all merchants are hereby ordered to comply. The original letter stated: "Gentlemen, our industry's request to cancel the extra charges is out of dire necessity. However, our industry's general assembly has resolved to comply despite reservations. According to the Nanshi side, these extra charges amount to only 23 cents per pig, with no pier fees or shop commissions. Now, your charges are 47 cents per pig, a significant difference. We request that you follow the same practices as your counterparts in Nanshi; otherwise, they will not be recognized at settlement. This letter is sent accordingly. We hope you will investigate and reply."

Ministry of Railways Instructs Railways to Print Valid Times on Joint Transport Round-Trip Tourist Tickets to Avoid Disputes 163

The two Railway Administrations received an instruction from the Ministry of Railways yesterday stating, "According to the report of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Administration Committee, General Letter No. 1274, dated March 30 of this year, although the final hour of the validity period of joint transport round-trip tourist tickets has been publicized to passengers using billboards in accordance with the resolution of the 17th National Joint Transport Conference, misunderstandings still frequently occur recently. In order to avoid disputes, it is proposed to print the valid time in addition to the 'valid for several days from the date of sale' wording already on the ticket. Please approve." It was found that the request to print the valid time on the joint transport round-trip tourist ticket is intended to avoid disputes and should be approved. Other passenger tickets of a similar nature should also be handled in the same way to ensure uniformity. The wording to be added is as follows: "The journey must be completed before midnight on the last day; otherwise, a supplementary ticket must be purchased." In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued for compliance. The bureau has already forwarded the order to the Traffic Department for compliance.

Chevrolet Passenger Cars Again Lead Sales in 1934 165

According to the official report of the Polk Company of America, after the efforts of November and December of last year, Chevrolet passenger cars once again led sales in 1934, exceeding the full-year sales of all other automobiles. The total number of sales for the year was 534,906 vehicles. At the end of October last year, Chevrolet passenger cars were more than 20,000 vehicles behind their main competitor. However, after selling more than 36,000 vehicles in November and more than 25,000 vehicles in December, they ultimately exceeded their biggest competitor by 11,675 vehicles. 1934 was the fourth consecutive year that Chevrolet passenger cars led sales and the sixth time in the last eight years. Chevrolet truck sales totaled 157,507 vehicles, also the highest of any brand. In 1934, Chevrolet's total sales of all types of vehicles were 692,413 vehicles, an increase of 118,040 vehicles compared to last year, with passenger car sales increasing by 60,413 vehicles and truck sales increasing by 57,617 vehicles. Chevrolet's ability to remain in the top spot last year was indeed due to its exceptional performance in the last six months of the year. While other manufacturers only sold 35% of their full-year sales during this period, Chevrolet was able to sell 49% of its full-year sales.

Red Cross Ends Refugee Camp for Songjiang Disaster Victims 173

Zhou Xuewen Arrives in Shanghai to Negotiate. Over 5,000 Yuan in Relief Funds Needed.

Last year, Zhejiang Province suffered from a severe drought, resulting in crop failure. The five counties of Haining, Jiaxing, Haiyan, Chongde, and Tongxiang were particularly affected. Disaster victims flocked to neighboring areas to beg for food. Songjiang, which is connected to Zhejiang Province, was the first to bear the brunt. People of all ages lined the streets, causing not only a public order concern but also something that benevolent people could not bear to see. Zhou Xuewen, Chairman of the Songjiang Branch of the Red Cross, proposed that the association set up a camp to accommodate them. For three months, the camp accommodated over 16,000 people, consuming over 1,200 dan of rice. When they were sent off, each person was given cash. The camp had already closed last month, but refugees from Jiaxing and Jiashan continued to arrive in hopes of finding shelter. The association could not bear to see them abandoned by the roadside and reluctantly provided accommodation again, but finances were strained. Chu Huiseng from the All-Zhejiang Drought Relief Association sent personnel to distribute over 3,000 rice vouchers, and the Shanghai Provincial Drought Relief Association distributed 1,200 relief vouchers, totaling 1,200 dan of rice. The cost of other expenses such as medicine and timber was not insignificant. The camp has now been completely closed. It is estimated that over 5,000 yuan is needed. The association held its tenth economic review meeting at Chao Guo Temple the other day and resolved to request a subsidy from the general association and to reward the personnel who had worked hard. Yesterday, Chairman Zhou came to Shanghai from Songjiang to report to the general association and to contact major philanthropists in Shanghai to solicit donations.

Ruling on盛毓常 (Shèng Yùcháng)'s Case of Being Sued by a Concubine: Sentence of Six Months, Suspended for Two Years 179

盛毓常 (Shèng Yùcháng), the eldest grandson of盛否蓀 (Shèng Fǒusūn), a former Palace Guardian and Minister of Posts and Communications in the late Qing Dynasty, originally from Changzhou, lived at No. 1, Danglu Road. Previously, through the introduction of his friend 苏石痴 (Sū Shíchī), he took 林玉金 (Lín Yùjīn), a Guangdong woman and prostitute, as a concubine. Later, because Lin (林) could not bear the schemes and oppression of Sheng's (盛) wife, she left on her own accord. For several years, due to the pressures of life, she worked as a dancer in the dance halls of Shanghai. After January 28th (referring to the Shanghai Incident of 1932), Sheng (盛) went to the dance hall to dance, and upon seeing Lin (林) again, he was reminded of their past affection. He generously agreed to take her back, renting a house downstairs at No. 191, Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, and they lived together again. Starting around April of last year, because Lin Yujin (林玉金) suffered from lung disease, Sheng (盛) suddenly abandoned her, disappearing completely. Lin (林) searched for Sheng (盛) several times but could not meet him. Helpless, Lin (林) engaged 江一平 (Jiāng Yīpíng), 华懋生 (Huá Màoshēng), and other lawyers to file a private prosecution against Sheng Yuchang (盛毓常) in the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court for abandonment. Based on the complaint, the court, through 章朝佐 (Zhāng Cháozuǒ), held several hearings, summoning both parties for interrogation and ordering Lin (林) to undergo a medical examination at the forensic medical office, confirming that she was suffering from lung and heart disease. The court adjourned the hearing and instructed both parties to attempt an out-of-court settlement. Subsequently, because the settlement failed, another hearing was held on the 4th of this month to continue the trial. The plaintiff, Lin Yujin (林玉金), suddenly requested to withdraw the attached civil suit, demanding that the criminal portion of the lawsuit be strictly handled according to the law against the defendant's abandonment. The defendant also engaged lawyers 山律 (Shān Lǜ) and 张鼎 (Zhāng Dǐng) for defense. The court instructed the lawyers of both parties to present their arguments, then announced the conclusion of the hearing and set a date for the verdict. Details of the case have been previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date set for the verdict in this case. Both parties were represented by their lawyers who came to the court to await the outcome. Judge 章 (Zhāng) presided over the Fourth Criminal Division and delivered the judgment, stating that Sheng Yuchang (盛毓常) had abandoned a person without the ability to support themselves, whom he was legally obligated to support. He was sentenced to six months of imprisonment, with a two-year suspended sentence. After the verdict, the official briefly explained the reasoning behind the judgment and then adjourned the court.

Judgment on Illegal Driver Density Case of祥生 (Xiángshēng) Motor Company 180

Previously, a strike wave occurred at the 祥生 (Xiángshēng) Motor Company. Man and Woman Imprisoned for Two Months Each for Adultery 181

杨国信 (Yáng Guóxìn), a Chinese constable with badge number 652 from Hebei Province at the Avenue Joffre Police Station, is 36 years old and lives at No. 46, Huaxing Fang, Baoding Road. In the fourth month of the lunar calendar two years ago, he married a woman from the same hometown, 阎氏 (Yánshì) (20 years old). However, before several months had passed, 阎氏 (Yánshì) suddenly left without notice, and her whereabouts were unknown. She also took away clothing and other items. Yang (杨) reported this to the Yangshupeilu Police Station. In May of last year, Yang (杨) learned that 阎氏 (Yánshì) was cohabitating with 左荣昌 (Zuǒ Róngchāng) at No. 9, Shuifu Li, Sanyang Road. He often went to arrest them, taking them to the police station, but they were dispersed after the police officer mediated. Then, as soon as 阎氏 (Yánshì) left the police station, she refused to go home with Yang (杨), claiming she was returning to her mother's home, and disappeared from then on. On the first of this month, Yang (杨) suddenly received an anonymous letter reporting that 阎氏 (Yánshì) was cohabitating with 蔡德和 (Cài Déhé), a man from Yangzhou, at No. 390, Zhoujiazui Road. After investigation, the report was confirmed. He reported it to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. Chinese detective 吕寿昌 (Lǚ Shòuchāng), along with Chinese constable No. 2723, rushed to the scene and arrested 阎氏 (Yánshì) and 蔡 (Cài), taking them to the police station. Cai (蔡) and 闫氏 (Yánshì) completely confessed to the facts of their adultery, and stated that they had initially cohabitated at No. 16, Wuyixing Li, Tongzhou. Since the detectives knew that they had a fixed residence, they immediately released them. Then, they requested the First Special District Court to issue a summons, and this morning Cai (蔡) and 阎氏 (Yánshì) were summoned to the Fifth Criminal Division. Police Lawyer 蒋保廉 (Jiǎng Bǎolián) prosecuted them for adultery under Article 256 of the Criminal Law. When questioned, Yang (杨) and 阎氏 (Yánshì) stated: "After marrying the plaintiff, the defendant (Yang) did not often come home because he thought I was ugly. My departure was forced by the plaintiff. After leaving, I made a living by washing clothes. However, I was heavily in debt. I met Cai (蔡) through washing clothes. Cai (蔡) paid off my debts for me, so I offered myself to him. We have been together for only five months." Cai Dehe's (蔡德和) statement was similar to Yan's (阎). After verifying their statements, Judge 叶圣超 (Yè Shèngchāo) declared in court that Yang (杨) 阎氏 (Yánshì) and 蔡德和 (Cài Déhé) would each be sentenced to two months of imprisonment as a warning.

Red Swastika Society Organizes Emergency Relief for Anhui Province: A Large Number of Relief Workers Depart 184

The disaster situation in Anhui Province is dire, with widespread famine. Many people are using Guanyin powder, tree bark, and grass roots as food, causing their bodies to swell and becoming weak and unable to move. There are even reports of parents and children eating each other. These tragic situations are heartbreaking. Previously, the Southeast Branches of the Red Swastika Society and the Shanghai United Office jointly raised over 10,000 yuan in relief funds with branches in Qing, Xi, Chang, Yong and other places. They publicly appointed Zhou Genjing (周根净) and Liu Xichun (柳锡纯) as supervisors and convened a meeting in Anqing to organize an emergency relief society, allocate relief funds, and elect relief workers to go to Hefei and other counties to provide emergency relief. The counties being inspected by the society are listed below: Hefei County: Yuan Zantai (袁赞太), Wu Yuande (吴圆德); Guichi County: Dai Fu Yin (戴肤因), Liu Zhen (刘　眞); Dangtu County: Zhen Hua (　振华), Shi Yuanyuan (十元境); Tongcheng County: Shi Miaole (施妙乐), You You (　悠　); Wangjiang County: He Huili (何惠利), Wu Wuhe (吴呜和); Huaining County: Wu Ying (吴　　影), Hao Cheng (郝　成); Fanchang County: Liu Zhenyuan (刘珍源), Xin Shouyi (辛守依); Susong and Taihe Counties: Zhou Juesi (周觉蕬), Liu Shoujue (刘守觉); Dongliu County: Sun Gu (孙　榖), Wang Shou (王守　); Shidai, Qingyang, and Tongling Counties: Yue Qing (　月清), Gao Deyuan (高德源), Zhang Suding (张素定), Xu Shouhuan (徐守焕); Hanzhen County: Shen Zhongchong (沈钟冲), Zhou Yujue (周毓觉); Xuancheng, Langxi, Nanling, and Jing County: Shi Zhidao (十志道), Chen Kaicheng (陈开成); Qianyou County: Hunfa (　浑法), Shi Hunjian (石浑见). In addition, 1,000 yuan was subsidized for the Sanhe Congee Kitchen, and 500 yuan each was given to the Huoqiu and Lujiang Counties, to be distributed by the society's North Anhui office. It is also reported that all branches have been telegraphed to raise funds together in order to expand relief efforts. However, there has been excessive rainfall in the province recently, and most of the wheat crop has been damaged. According to relief workers, lives cannot be saved until the autumn grain harvest. The society's relief funds are limited, and it is hoped that benevolent people from all walks of life will raise funds to save the starving people from death. One yuan can save one life, and the merit is greater than building a pagoda.

Jiangsu Provincial Party Committee: Zhou Houjun Comes to Shanghai to Raise Relief Funds; Mayor Wu and Others Enthusiastically Support 185

Zhou Houjun, a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Committee, convened a relief meeting in Zhenjiang with representatives from the county governments, county party committees, farmers' associations, chambers of commerce, drought relief associations, and local charitable individuals from ten counties, including Liyang, Lishui, Jurong, Liuhe, Jintan, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Yixing, and Yizheng, due to the severe disaster situation. Zhou recently came to Shanghai to solicit donations. The reporter visited him and recorded his remarks as follows: In recent years, our country's rural areas have suffered from frequent natural and man-made disasters, compounded by the economic aggression of imperialists, and are teetering on the brink of collapse, a situation too painful to mention. Jiangsu is known as a fertile region, but even there, nine out of ten homes are empty and few families have any savings. Last year's severe drought was a calamity unprecedented in a century. The situation in counties such as Yi and Li, due to their high terrain, was even more severe. Ponds and lakes dried up day by day. The cracks in the ground were wide enough for carriages and horses to travel through. It is impossible to discuss planting, let alone harvesting crops. The farmers, seeing that there was no hope for survival, fled in all directions, eating in the wind and sleeping in the dew, selling their children and daughters. Now that the spring plowing season has arrived, they have returned crawling to their fields. However, when they inspect the fields, they have nothing to plow with, and after the drought, they have exhausted all their resources and have nothing to eat. They are digging up graves to eat corpses, swallowing stones to commit suicide, and starving corpses fill the fields. Their crying shakes the heavens. Houjun has been traveling to various places and has seen and heard these things with his own eyes. His heart is broken. Therefore, he convened a drought relief meeting of ten counties. Chairman Chen of the provincial government has decided to establish a poor people's loan office in each county to provide full relief efforts. The provincial party committee also plans to allocate the funds raised by party members in the past to relief efforts. However, the disaster area is tens of thousands of square miles wide, and the disaster victims number over a million. This is still a drop in the bucket and difficult to make a difference. Houjun has come to Shanghai to appeal for help. Fortunately, Mr. Wu Tiecheng, Xu Shiying, Du Yuesheng, Gu Xingxuan, Huang Jinrong, Wu Kaixian, Wu Xingya, and Pan Gongzhan have enthusiastically supported him. The Drought Relief Association and the Municipal Government have allocated 10,000 yuan, which will be sent this Saturday. Mr. Du Yuesheng and Wu Xingya have also agreed to personally solicit donations. These gentlemen, who are concerned about the suffering of others and have a charitable heart, are not only the saviors of the disaster victims in the ten counties of Yi and Li, but also the pillars of the nation and deeply worthy of respect. Zhou was very saddened when he spoke and also said that one yuan is enough to save a life. He sincerely hoped that the people of the metropolis would tighten their belts and rise up to provide disaster relief.

Penalties for Selling Poisonous Substances Recorded 190

(1) Wang Qingfang, a Shandong native, was found by Detective Shen Kui of the Huizhaifang Police Station at around 9:00 PM the day before yesterday selling smuggled red pills, about 60, and a small packet of heroin powder near Sanguantang on Huazhai Road. Because he looked suspicious, they knew he was a red pill peddler. They bought a packet from him for five jiao and arrested him, along with the evidence, and took him to the police station. The police chief ordered him to be detained. Yesterday, he was brought before the Third Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Industry Bureau Lawyer Li Zhishan stated the facts and filed a public prosecution under Article 6 of the Drug Prohibition Law. He requested the court to present the red pills and heroin powder for inspection and to question the defendant. The defendant's testimony was evasive. Judge Zizi sentenced Wang Qingfang to six months in prison as a warning and ordered the confiscation and destruction of the evidence. Dancer's Abortion Death Case: Further Interrogation Awaits Witness Summons 191

Chen Weida, the owner of the Weida Hotel at No. 993 Avenue Joffre and a native of Nantong, had a relationship with the dancer Bao Yuying, a native of Xuzhou. The woman was secretly pregnant and was worried about her dancing career. On March 4th of this year, she went to the old midwife Liu Wang at No. 73 Jiujiang Road for an abortion. Afterwards, she suffered internal injuries and became ill. Her father, Bao Zhenyuan, learned that she had become ill because of the pregnancy and abortion related to Chen. She was then sent to Guangren Hospital, but treatment was ineffective and she died on the 11th of the same month. Now, the woman's father, Bao Zhenyuan, has engaged a lawyer to file a private prosecution in the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court against Chen Weida for inducing fornication and hindering public morals. After Judge Li Changnian of the First Special Court held a hearing on October 25th, he ordered a change of date, pending the collection of the case file of Liu Wang from the First Special Court for review and summons of witnesses for further interrogation, as previously reported. Yesterday, another hearing was held and both parties were represented by lawyers. The official first briefly questioned both parties and then summoned Wu Changkai, a detective from the Xinzha Police Station, to the stand. After ordering him to take an oath, Wu testified that on March 11th, he was on duty at the Xinzha Police Station. At 5:00 PM, he received a phone call from Guangren Hospital reporting an abortion case involving a woman named Bao Huiying. The police chief immediately sent him to Guangren Hospital to investigate. According to Bao, she was still a Miss, not married. He asked her since she was not married, how did she get pregnant? She said she had a lover named Chen who ran a hotel on Avenue Joffre, but refused to say Chen's name, and asked him to ask her father, etc. He then returned to the police station to report. At 6:20 PM, Guangren Hospital called again, saying that Bao Huiying had died. He and a Western detective went to the Public Security Bureau on North Sichuan Road and notified the woman's father, Bao Zhenyuan. Later, because the abortion midwife lived next door to the Big Dance Hall on Sanma Road and was under the jurisdiction of the Laozha Police Station, the police chief transferred the case to the Laozha Police Station for handling. When he was inquiring about Bao Huiying at Guangren Hospital, there was also a doctor surnamed Yu standing by, listening to the conversation. The defendant absolutely denied having a relationship with Bao Huiying, saying that he had known her since last June when she was dancing. The witnesses Bai Xiuzhen and the maid Wang Amei had not arrived. According to the plaintiff Bao Zhenyuan, the witness Wang Amei has returned to her hometown of Lumu in Suzhou, and he has sent a letter to notify Bai Xiuzhen that he knows that his daughter and Chen were opening rooms at the Zha Hotel. The plaintiff's attorney requested a change of date and that the plaintiff be allowed to summon the witnesses for further interrogation. The court verified the statement and ordered a postponement until the third day of the month to summon the witnesses for questioning.

Food Stall Vendor Deceived, Angered and Stabs Abdomen with Cleaver 192

Zhang Ziluo, a local man, 48 years old, rents No. 44, Lane 149, Changsha Road, and runs a food stall for a living, which is barely enough to maintain his livelihood and save a little. A friend, Mr. Jia, came to him and said that a certain small transportation business was in need of a cook, which would be very profitable. Zhang, blinded by greed, closed his food stall and went to take the job. The friend took the opportunity to swindle all his money, and soon he was fired from his job. Later, his family reported to the police station, and Officer No. 71 went to investigate and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment. His wife was brought to the Gangbu Police Station for questioning.

Special Article

Business Report of the Bank of Communications (12) 200

(5) Commercial Acceptance and Discount: The Bank has been working hard to promote this for several years, but unfortunately, it has not been fully implemented at the beginning. Now, the general society has seen the necessity of promoting and implementing acceptance and discount methods. In the future, we plan to actively carry out this policy to increase the number of chips in the market to maximize the benefits of turnover and circulation.

(6) Seek Close Cooperation among Banking Colleagues: The trend from competition to cooperation among banking colleagues is a major change in recent times, as mentioned earlier. Various production enterprises need funds. Taking cotton as an example, in the 23rd year, the national cotton production is estimated to produce more than 11 million dan of lint. At 40 yuan per dan, it requires more than 440 million yuan in funds. Other domestic raw materials are combined for calculation, and the amount of funds needed is even greater. Therefore, in terms of the amount of funds, if banks work together, they are still worried about the need for more supply and less demand, and there is no need for competition. There are also various specialized talents in business that are also extremely needed, but there are insufficient allocations. Furthermore, the equipment such as warehouses is handled by each bank individually, which is inevitably redundant and extremely uneconomical. Therefore, if they can cooperate effectively, not only will all investments be safe, but they will also be more in line with economic principles. The various cooperative businesses that were handled this year have been quite effective. In the future, we should still adhere to the main purpose of the group and seek closer cooperation. On the one hand, we should increase the types and scope of cooperative businesses. Those that are not suitable for cooperative methods should also be handled with a coordinated attitude.

The above are all business-related matters. There are also personnel and management aspects, such as talent cultivation, division of labor, and regional management, which should also be planned to make them suitable for the progress of business.

Conclusion

Judging from the situation in all aspects, the economic undertakings of our country have reached a critical juncture of life and death. The whole country, especially the financial world, should have a deep understanding and thorough awareness, stand firm, do practical work, and do our part. Regarding investment business, we must be able to divide the work and also be able to cooperate. It is not appropriate to engage in useless competition, and it is especially important to avoid everyone rushing to the same path. In other words, we should make planned investments. On the one hand, we should use the development of strength economically, and the allocation of chips should also be carefully planned. On the other hand, we should provide loans for production according to our ability, appropriately reduce deposit and loan interest rates, and support agriculture, while still promoting the development of industry, implementing production control, and preventing excessive price increases. In addition, we hope that (1) transportation will be developed, safety will be guaranteed, and taxes will be reduced, (2) land transportation costs will be reduced, and we will continue to strive for simplification, (3) industrial and commercial management will be scientific, and production and sales undertakings will be rationalized. The fundamental key lies in the people of the country doing their best and cooperating effectively, not relying on the assistance of others, not seeking temporary benefits, eliminating emotional effects, and promoting domestic production. Internal difficulties may be resolved, and external oppression may be avoided. The future is bright, and the prosperity of the banking business is also in this. How can it only be the bank's responsibility? (End)

Educational News

Siamese Minister of Education Explains Absurd Statement on Suppressing Chinese Schools 201

Reclaiming Forced Classes and Prohibiting Teaching of Party Doctrine - Weak in the Face of the Strong and No Restrictions on Other Countries

Bai Shangshalapapan, the Siamese Minister of Education, has caused unanimous opposition from overseas Chinese due to the implementation of assimilation policies by suppressing Chinese schools, which has led to many questions. However, the minister has resorted to sophistry and issued a statement explaining the suppression of Chinese schools, which is extremely absurd and infuriating. The reporter of the Industry and Commerce Society has specially transcribed the original text of the statement as follows:

Unwilling to Allow Other Countries to Seize Educational Power

(1) The principle of education is that each country has the sovereignty to achieve its educational goals and is unwilling to allow the people of other countries to arbitrarily and privately have the special right to run education. Similarly, China is the same as Siam. The same formula is to preserve the sovereignty of implementing education in the country and not allow overseas Chinese (no matter whether they are overseas Chinese or overseas Chinese from other countries who have this kind of special right). (2) The implementation law of education in Siam has been clearly promulgated, and there are laws and regulations related to the implementation of education, namely (A) the Private School Regulations (Buddhist calendar 1461), (B) the Compulsory Education Regulations (Buddhist calendar 464).

Turning the Compulsory Classes to Be Run by the Ministry

(3) All private schools, whether they are Chinese schools, Siamese schools, or schools founded by overseas Chinese from other countries, should be run in accordance with the above-mentioned education regulations. The Ministry of Education has not strictly restricted the schools, such as allowing Chinese schools to teach the courses stipulated by the Ministry of Education. In the past, the Ministry of Education also allowed Chinese teachers who had not participated in Siamese language training to serve as teachers during school learning time, so that the schools could be maintained to this day. This kind of thing shows that Chinese schools enjoy special rights more than Siamese schools. The Ministry of Education also takes a tolerant attitude towards the management of private schools. For example, if Chinese schools have mistakes, they are treated with the same attitude. The Ministry of Education is infinitely grateful for the good intentions of the Chinese directors and teachers for establishing schools in the country and enlightening the children of the country (the children enrolled by the Chinese are all children of overseas Chinese) and being able to consistently do good deeds to this day. Therefore, the Ministry of Education often provides various conveniences within the scope of the law, but when there is no way to forgive, I hope that the Chinese and Chinese schools can understand that the Ministry of Education should not have an attitude of only caring about one side.

Forcing Chinese Children to Learn Siamese

(4) When compulsory education is promulgated and implemented in various places, it is implemented in accordance with the regulations. Except for the districts where the Ministry of Education has raised the compulsory age to eight or nine years old, all boys and girls within the compulsory age, from seven to fourteen years old, should attend classes in compulsory schools (that is, schools run by Siam) and go to school in accordance with the compulsory education regulations. This is the principle of Siam implementing compulsory education. Therefore, in the areas where compulsory education regulations have been promulgated, private schools of overseas Chinese from various countries, if they want to enroll children of compulsory age, must be in accordance with the provisions of various compulsory education regulations and teach according to the compulsory education curriculum. As for the Chinese schools, because a foreign language subject (that is, Chinese and English) is inserted in the middle of the curriculum, if the compulsory education regulations are strictly implemented, the Chinese schools will not be allowed to enroll children of compulsory age (that is, Chinese children aged seven to fourteen). However, the Ministry of Education has not forgotten the good intentions of the Chinese schools in Siam and education, so it allows the Chinese schools to adopt courses equivalent to the compulsory education curriculum and allows them to teach in foreign languages. This can be said to be a special courtesy of the Ministry of Education to all Chinese schools in the country.

Not Allowed to Teach Party Doctrine Textbooks

(5) If the Chinese schools can abide by the implementation of the Ministry of Education and the education regulations, they will be given various benefits and receive considerable assistance from the Ministry of Education. However, the fact is not the case. Most Chinese schools take advantage of this opportunity to teach various other courses and political doctrines (that is, the Three Principles of the People textbook) and do not teach courses related to various appropriate courses, such as vocational education or other courses. The teaching of political doctrines is not within the scope of courtesy. Therefore, the Ministry of Education, which is responsible for organizing education and maintaining common interests, has to stop this kind of treatment for the schools. (6) The above-mentioned non-compliant actions of the Chinese schools will inevitably affect the inability of children to achieve the goals of the compulsory regulations. In order to seek common interests and enforce the law, the Ministry of Education has no choice but to withdraw the education power. (The Chinese schools enroll children of overseas Chinese, and there are no Siamese children in them. The Ministry's withdrawal of education power is even the education power of China,) It is absurd to withdraw it together.)

British, French, and Other Overseas Chinese Are Not Subject to This Example

(7) As for the actual situation of the schools violating the regulations, after questioning some of the directors who run the Chinese schools, it was found that the purpose of establishing the Chinese schools was only to enable children to learn Chinese. If teachers teach students political doctrines, they are also dissatisfied and even disappointed. This investigation result shows that some of the directors of the schools have not participated in this illegal behavior. The Ministry of Education is very grateful for this kind of good intention and hopes that other directors of the schools can understand this matter and cooperate with the Ministry of Education so that this matter can achieve a complete result in accordance with the provisions of the compulsory education regulations. This shows that the Ministry of Education has not, as the general rumors say, implemented the closure of Chinese schools and hindered the behavior of Chinese children from reading Chinese. On the contrary, the Ministry of Education will find ways to enable the children of all Chinese to read Chinese. Even Siamese children have the opportunity to learn Chinese. For example, in order to facilitate some merchants, the Ministry of Education also has a Chinese language course in schools run by the government. All Chinese who have lived in Siam for a long time and newcomers enjoy the same treatment as Siamese under the same law and the same regulations. (Overseas Chinese from Britain, France, the United States, and Japan who live in Siam are generally not subject to this treatment by the Siamese government.) The Dong schools and Siamese schools are prescribed in the same law, and Chinese schools should enjoy various special conveniences such as those mentioned above compared to other Siamese schools.

Restrictions on the Use of the Chinese Language

The restricted use of the Chinese language is what the Ministry of Education should pay special attention to in the management of education in Siam. For the education of children of compulsory age, and those under the compulsory education age or have exceeded the compulsory education age, the private schools may teach foreign languages in accordance with the provisions of the National School Regulations. This has been given considerable rights. The Ministry of Education has stated above that it allows the Chinese schools to use courses equivalent to the compulsory education curriculum and allows them to use foreign languages (that is, use the Chinese language) for teaching. However, this is only a courtesy outside the law and is actually an aid in the early stages of the schools. However, later it was felt that this kind of treasure was used by the schools to teach political doctrines, which violated the compulsory education regulations. Therefore, the Ministry of Education took on the actual responsibility of management so that it could be implemented in accordance with the regulations. If the schools can run in accordance with the laws, the Ministry of Education officials will give them various conveniences. According to the above reasons, all Siamese and Chinese believe that the Ministry of Education's withdrawal of education power this time is based on legal principles and there is no forced behavior. The Ministry of Education is responsible for the management of national education, so it has to be responsible for preserving and maintaining it, so that it can be implemented in accordance with the track of the compulsory regulations and the national education policy, and achieve perfection, hoping that students can understand their responsibilities and seek development for themselves, their country, nation, religion, and constitution.

A Stream of New World Records

TASS, Moscow, 8th – A female Soviet athlete set a new backstroke swimming record yesterday. She swam 400 meters in 6 minutes and 7.2 seconds, breaking the previous record of 6 minutes and 12.4 seconds held by English swimmer Ms. Gralla.

Meanwhile, Zhongfa School's team performed calisthenics, which were orderly, lively, and exceptionally beautiful. Finally, honorary president Lu Bohong and Shen Yuguang presented awards, and the event concluded at dusk.

Overview of Track and Field

In the track and field events, Zhao Jialiang of Zhongfa demonstrated a tight and fierce running style in the 100 meters, proving to be a promising talent. Ma Juncai's 400 meters featured wide strides and consistency throughout, with a particularly strong sprint at the finish line, resulting in a time of 56.5 seconds. In the 1500 meters, St. Francis' young Zhang Liang, originally a leading figure, performed less impressively than usual with a time of 4 minutes and 39 seconds due to a lack of competition. In the high jump, Wu Guangtao of Zhongfa's Group A achieved a height of 1.68 meters, and it is said that he can usually jump 1.73 meters, indicating a promising future. The competition results showed Zhongfa sweeping the championships in Groups A, B, and C, winning the overall championship. St. Francis took second place, Jin Ke third, and Zhengxiu scored the least, placing fourth. The results are listed below:

First District Elementary School Sports Meet Holds Second Preparatory Meeting Yesterday 223

Gu Yinqian and others elected to the presidium of the conference

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is hosting this year's District Elementary School Joint Sports Meet, scheduled to begin tomorrow in the Eighth District. It has been learned that the Preparatory Committee for the First District held its second meeting yesterday at the Municipal Sports Field. All members of the Preparatory Committee attended, with Gu Yinqian presiding and Jiang Yuanheng as the secretary. Wang Keshui represented the Education Bureau. The following matters were resolved: (1) Regarding the requirement for schools to submit photos of athletes when registering, it was decided to issue a separate explanatory note when schools pick up the forms. (2) Regarding whether the estimated budget for this sports meet should be adjusted, it was decided to follow the Education Bureau's specified budget and transfer the budget reduction for the running track and command platform to miscellaneous expenses and printing. (3) Regarding whether a specialist should be assigned to take photos of the winning athletes, it was decided to send a letter to Chai Zifei to undertake this task. (4) Regarding the election of the conference presidium, it was decided to elect Gu Yinqian, Wang Dingcheng, Xu Peihang, Tang Guodong, and Yao Jilang as the five members. (5) Regarding whether a military band should be invited to play at the opening ceremony, it was decided to send a letter to the Poor Children's Home band to perform. (6) Regarding how to solicit awards for the conference from various sectors, it was decided to send letters to various organizations to request donations for promotion and to invite representatives from various organizations to attend the conference. (7) Regarding the designation of a resting area for the athletes and a camping area for the Boy Scouts, it was decided to designate the gymnasium as the athletes' resting area. If schools wish to build their own shelters, they should be limited to the basketball court in front of the gymnasium. The camping area for the Boy Scouts should be limited to the tennis court and the playground of the Changru Department. (8) Regarding the regulations for badges for the conference staff and referees, it was decided that staff from the administrative department will use yellow badges, and staff from the competition department will use red badges. The meeting was adjourned.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 228

— (Shadow Dun)

The greatest hydraulic force in the world - is a woman's tears. The rest of the new era is just when the old era rises again.

If you are laughing, the world is also laughing at you; if you are crying, then you are ruining the development of your future.

The more wills you write, the more lawsuits there will be.

There are many stages on the ladder of reputation.

Although some women like modern men, most women still like old-fashioned men.

A father of the times should not care about the income and expenses of his children.

In the spring, what a young man fantasizes about is everything a young woman has fantasized about in the winter.

Fingerprints 229

— Qing Qu

The organization of Baojia (neighborhood watch system) is meant to train the populace to collectively organize for self-defense. Since its implementation, I've heard that the local organization of youth matters is progressing smoothly. However, there is one matter in the current third phase of work that the common people do not quite understand. That is, on the joint guarantee form, the Jia head and household head should both press their "fingerprints." Because of this, the gentlemen serving as Bao heads are suffering, spending much effort on promotion and persuasion. Those who are shrewd and clever, knowing the difficulties of the task, rush to resign in order to avoid trouble. What is the reason? When the villagers hear that they have to press "fingerprints," they are all terrified, saying, "We have not committed any crimes, nor have we engaged in selling wives and children. Why should we press 'fingerprints' and suffer this humiliation?" From this, it can be seen that the nation has not yet reached a sufficient level. It is truly not easy to implement the country's laws and decrees to the entire populace and to deeply ingrain them into the minds of the majority.

Speaking of the countryside, this is indeed the case. But if we look at the city, then it's completely different! For example, in our Jiading area, several Bao heads in the city, perhaps suspecting that some people are doubtful and hesitant, press their own "fingerprints" first to promote it. So yesterday, I saw several joint forms covered with "fingerprints," which was quite a sight to behold. Those trying to avoid it privately are truly a minority. This is perhaps a difference between the city and the countryside! But the "fingerprints" that are pressed, it's a pity that there is little research done on them. Natural ink is used, but because the texture is too heavy, it's either too dry or too wet. Some people press too hard, resulting in a blurry ink mess, not only failing to show the lines, but even tearing the paper when the finger is lifted. Pressing too lightly, on the other hand, doesn't even leave a mark on the paper. Moreover, the grid on the joint form is very narrow. Under a household head's name, if you just press randomly, wouldn't that cause confusion? Therefore, after seeing this procedure, I am reminded that the science of fingerprinting should also be studied. If there is no experience, a sudden attempt to implement it will inevitably feel somewhat lacking.

Eulogy for Mr. Yang Dunfu 230

— Tian Xu Wo Sheng

Mr. Yang Dunfu supported me from the time I founded the family industrial cooperative, and was especially close to Xiaodie. The night talk with wine in the Zui Ling Xuan two years ago further revealed his ancient spirit. Now that he has returned to Dao Mountain, I first offer two elegiac couplets on behalf of my two brothers, Xiaochao and Zongcheng, this is the sorrow after three sighs.

Words cannot fully express my feelings, may his spirit be aware.

We knew each other for two generations, eighteen years of fleeting time, but in recent years, I often lamented that meetings were few and separations were many, let alone being separated by death from now on.

I toil with a cup of sorrowful elegy, tracing back the 5,000 words of morality, and wanting to express myself fully, I always feel that affection is long and paper is short, is it possible to share a cup of wine again?

Elegiac couplet on behalf of Mr. Jin Zongcheng

I worked with you for more than twenty years, correcting my faults like a father and son, reducing my mistakes like a sage, upright, honest and knowledgeable, I have benefited indeed not shallowly. Who knew that destiny is hard to defy, a long life of one hundred and eight years is only halfway through.

Thirteen years older than me, your dignity like a teacher and friend, your affection like brothers, good and bad you always discerned, our mutual understanding only grew deeper. Who would have thought that saying goodbye on Sunday, the thousands of treasured moments would end in a long farewell.

Elegiac couplet on behalf of Brother Tu Xiaochao

We became friends in childhood, forty-eight years until now, relying on each other like jade trees. Unexpectedly, minor misfortune occurred, and from then on, immortals and mortals are eternally separated.

We shared hearts and were in harmony, more than two thousand days older than me, nurturing each other no different from sworn brothers. Thinking of the many troubles in the Central Plains, why not detach and rest in peace.

Du Juan's Note: Elegiac couplets are the most difficult to compose, valuing sincerity of feeling and clarity like spoken words, not to be used for others. Die Lao (Elder Butterfly) has long been skilled in this, but regrettably he has often not left drafts. Now these three couplets are all for one person, from one hand, but each has its own feelings, lingering with endless grief. As the poem says: "Others have intentions, I measure them," is this not what it means? Recently, couplets are often stiff and empty, I record this to show a model for scholars, or not to be嫌d for merely occupying space.

Returning to the Same Old Path 231

— Jiang Mi

Picking Roses 232

— (Bo Guang)

The long snake-like Ping Mountain ridge, stretches for tens of miles, planted all over with bright red roses. Many village girls, in twos and threes, huddle among the rose bushes, picking roses that are still budding.

The clear and warm sunlight, shining on their bodies, feels prickly and unbearable, so they have already stripped off their cotton jackets, leaving only a single shirt, which is still wet with sweat under their arms.

The color of the roses is so beautiful, set off by the deep green tender leaves, they appear even more delicate and charming; and there is a faint fragrance, how can one not love them.

Although they are village girls, some of them are symbolic of roses, with healthy bodies, innocent faces, shy expressions... In the rose-picking season, some frivolous young men from the neighborhood, especially run there, chatting with them with glib tongues and thick faces. The more experienced village girls scold them, isn't this like roses having thorns?

After the roses are picked, they are sold in whole loads to stores that specialize in collecting roses. But they originally have to go through the hands of female workers, dried and sorted. Then they are resold to pastry shops, candy shops, to be made into food, it is truly fragrant to eat.

Little Western Heaven 233

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 13: Arranging a Marriage is Difficult, Pitying Selling One's Body, Happily Serving as a Commodity, Going Bankrupt and Talking about Farmers

This county is even poorer than Shen County, and he was assigned to a township elementary school. The salary there is so small that it would make Westerners laugh their teeth out, it was originally two silver dollars a month. Zhou Yourong said: Although I have been in Shaanxi for so long, I did not expect elementary school teachers to have such hardship. But here there is a problem. May I ask, with two dollars a month, is it enough to drink water, enough to eat pot cakes? Even if he is very frugal, he definitely cannot teach on an empty stomach. Hokkaido: Naturally the salary is so low that it is only two dollars a month, we cannot ask the teacher to provide their own food. In fact, the food in the countryside is only two dollars a month. Altogether, including salary and food, it is about less than five dollars. May I ask, what kind of treatment is this? My relative taught for a semester, and felt that this was no different from begging for food. In the end, he resolutely resigned and quit. Zhi Qian said: He resigned and quit, did someone else take over? Hokkaido: Of course. Zhou Yourong laughed: Your relative is unwilling to beg for food, but others are willing to beg for food? Bei Hai laughed: Here there is naturally a qualification problem, my relative has after all spent two years in middle school, he felt that earning two dollars a month was not worth it. But there are those who have not entered the gate of middle school, they earn two dollars a month in the Northwest, then it is quite worth it. Zhi Qian said: You said those who have not entered the gate of middle school, can elementary school graduates also come out to be teachers? Bei Hai laughed: This must be said separately. It is certainly not very suitable to have not entered the gate of middle school, some have not even stepped into the gate of elementary school, and just know a few lines of poetry "Confucius said," and generally want to come out to teach. (201)

Records of the Lingering Fragrance of the Imperial Incense 234

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Everyone was wearing full court attire, as beautiful as a cluster of flowers, a pile of brocade; this scene, which I had long watched without getting tired of, but today I could not arouse any interest, on the contrary I felt that their actions were too slow, delaying our important matter of going to see the dogs, and I could not help but urge them loudly. I stole another glance at the Empress Dowager, only to see that she also seemed very anxious, speaking much more urgently than usual, all the memorials, she did not look at any of them in the court, only ordered the eunuchs to collect them and talk about it later.

However, this morning court could not be too hasty after all, it still had to take a considerable amount of time to end. After it was over, we all accompanied the Empress Dowager back to the inner palace together, first letting her hurriedly change into a set of lighter clothes for walking, and then everyone, according to the usual order, formed a scattered line, bustlingly crowding around the Empress Dowager, bypassed a corner of Longevity Hill, and went straight to the imperial doghouse. The location of this imperial doghouse was just to the left of the workshops of various artisans that I mentioned in the previous chapter, and it was closest to the silk-making workshop, but they were still one or two hundred paces apart! Along the way, the Empress Dowager also told me a lot about the situation of the dogs that we were going to visit now.

"Ah! Don't underestimate them too much!" This was one of the Empress Dowager's catchphrases, as if her things were all unbelievably great. "They also have a very long history: at first they also came from outside the pass like us, their original name was Haba dogs, this is the Manchurian local name, now very few people mention it." (311)

Miscellaneous Talk

Impressions of the Women's Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition 235

— Long Sao

The Chinese Women's Calligraphy and Painting Association has collected many works by purely female artists, and has been publicly exhibiting them at Lake Society these days. If we think about it in terms of its name, it is indeed worth our attention. In the ancient capital of culture—Beiping, in Guangzhou, the birthplace of revolution, in Wuhan, where higher education is active, in Hangzhou, the scenic traffic area, and in Kyoto, the center of political negotiation: it seems that we have not heard of any women who love calligraphy and painting organizing groups to study this kind of art. But now, the "Chinese Women's Calligraphy and Painting Association," centered on Shanghai, has gathered the artworks of women from all walks of life, and displayed them together in one place, which is really not an easy thing, especially since this is the first time!

It is not easy to produce a new art group and continue to operate with an independent spirit, completely maintained by women; as for the evaluation of their products, I personally think that it is not necessary to use modern trends to harshly say that they are too classicist, full of longing for hermit life, too lacking in social reality, and neglecting those noble nonsense of "the object of the masses" for the time being. Therefore, based on this position, I do not want to expound on modern art theory, but just want to simply talk about their products and style.

There: Like the landscape paintings of Zhu Renyan, Zhang Youfen, Huang Bingqing, Fan Songfen, and Xu Lengcui, they all rely on talent and skill, so the composition does not fall into fixed patterns. Gu Qingyao imitated Shi Xi in one painting and Xin Luo in six paintings, not only are they exquisite and profound, but the charming charm, like a light and agile wind, writes out her personal poetic feelings. Wu Qingxia's figures have the meaning of Huangshan Shou. Xie Yingxin's "Red Cliff Night Tour" and Bao Yahui's "Returning Home from Spring Outing" both have a fresh and elegant flavor. He Yiru imitated Da Chi, and Lu Xiaoman's small landscape painting is simply a work in the style of the Song and Yuan dynasties, like a beautiful palace poem, the posture is full of quiet leisure. Zhao Hanying, Liu Fangqiong, He Xiangning, and Jiang Yanan, etc., are all clear, elegant, vigorous, and the ink brush and coloring are all good. Li Qiujun's six-foot "Flower Shadow Blowing Sheng" and figure screen are painted in an antique, beautiful, bright, and well-proportioned layout. The landscapes she paints are also strangely comfortable to look at. Bao Qiongxiao and Mao Suihua's two paintings of beautiful women are elegant and delicate, and the landscapes are colored with blue and green, the method is close to Qiu Nong. Chen Xiaocui's "Wildcat Hunting Scroll," "Lychee Fragrance Near," and "Autumn Grave Ghost Singing Picture" needless to say have a graceful and refined charm, just like her poetic style; and she also writes a good hand of calligraphy. Tang Guanyu's flowers and birds, the brushwork is clear and refined. Ding Yunbi's grass insects, precisely because they are unkempt and roughly dressed, are even more beautiful and wonderful. Pang Zuoyu's "Willow Pond Picture" and "Late Autumn Picture" have the style of Bai Yang. Li Hua's White Eagle Picture is extremely ancient and elegant, I am afraid it cannot be regarded as a rare treasure in modern painting. Huang Quan's chrysanthemums, a total of twenty-four paintings, are vividly written and also rare and wonderful ink works. Zhou Lianxia's small painting of ink orchid is delicate and lovely, with inscriptions by Xiaocui, Qiujun, and Qingyao on it, it is indeed a collaborative masterpiece. Xu Hui's landscape three-foot screen, the ink rhyme is deep and moist, shining together with Jin Qiusheng and Yao Xinhua's clear, transcendent, simple and unadorned.

As for calligraphy, Feng Wenfeng has the most couplets, with great power. Jiang Daofan's seal or official script is also vigorously powerful. Wu Zhangzhu's imitation of Zhang Heinu is very similar in spirit, with only one work on display. Yang Xuejiu's three-foot screen, the ink is full and saturated, and the sweeping and dripping is almost no different from the wrist strength of a reckless man. In addition, Gu Qingyao's green stone seal carving and Zhang Renzhi's bamboo carving are also exhibited. Even if they are appendages, on this side seat, we can find their deep love for art. If we must find shortcomings, it lies in the fact that all the products inevitably fall into the consciousness of imitating the ancients, and neglect the spirit of modern artistic creation. It is hoped that the third exhibition will give us realistic portrayals that reflect real life and the fresh and lively stimulation of the progress of upward consciousness!

Telegrams from British and French firms have not brought any changes, and the local silk stocking factories are also very sluggish. Therefore, both the silk and silk fabric industries seem to be in a state of stagnation. The dying silk market is now only waiting for the excitement of new Xinjiang silk coming onto the market, which may be able to slightly invigorate it. However, it is also difficult to say.

Large Quantity of Keemun Black Tea Arrives in Shanghai 248

Yesterday, Zhongxin Chang, Yongxinglong, Qianji, and other tea warehouses transported 17 shipments of first-batch Keemun black tea from Hangzhou, totaling more than 1,300 boxes. Samples should be available today. The green tea market is trading quite actively. Zhuanmei green tea from the Suian road area is being heavily purchased by Xiehe, Yihuo, Jinlong, Tianwang, and other foreign firms due to the urgency of the shipping schedule. Zhuanmei green tea from local Zhuang, Huzhou, and other road areas is also being sold as soon as it arrives. The market price remains stable.

Piece Goods: Black Carbon Interlining is Expensive 249

Black carbon interlining, which is essential for the lapels and facing of Western suits, has seen a sharp reduction in the import of imported goods since the Ningbo Zishan interlining and the Shanghai Hongsheng Daohua products came out, resulting in rising market prices. This is what is meant by scarcity making things more expensive. Yesterday, the selling price of that black carbon increased sharply. A batch was sold at 1.45 yuan per yard, because the Teng Customs tariff moved to a weight-based tax, which amounts to about 6 jiao per yard, which made costs high, and the selling price was forced to become more expensive. Yesterday, Hongsheng black carbon sleeves sold for 1.35 yuan, and Jiangshan sold for 2.3 jiao.

Hardware: Hardware Prices Fall Across the Board 250

The hardware market has been unusually sluggish recently. The reason for this is the tight credit conditions. Purchases by foreign merchants have decreased, and many local factories have stopped operations. The market's turnover has therefore been sharply reduced, and the frequent arrivals of goods have caused fear. Only those in the industry with strong financial resources are trying their best to maintain the market, but unfortunately, prices are still falling gradually. Among all the hardware varieties, there is a loosening trend. The main varieties are recorded below:

Plain Galvanized Iron: Since Eastern goods flooded in, the market has been greatly affected. Although there is still some movement in the Yangtze River and other inland areas, most of it is scattered. The market sentiment is also affected by the loosening of foreign exchange, which makes it even more difficult to fill the gap. The current market price is estimated at 10.05 yuan per dan for No. 24, 11.5 yuan for No. 26, and 12.5 yuan for No. 28. American goods sell for 11.5 yuan per dan for No. 24, 12.5 yuan for No. 26, and 13.6 yuan for No. 28, a decrease of 2-3 jiao to 4-5 jiao compared to the previous price. It is said that only 100-200 bundles were traded in the market yesterday.

Galvanized Iron Sheet: The sales of this product made great progress in previous years, but now it is also going downhill due to the pressure of the poor environment. Although sellers are unwilling to loosen the market, prices are still tending to decline invisibly. The current market price is estimated at 11.25 yuan per dan for No. 24, 11.65 yuan for No. 26, and 12.55 yuan for No. 28, a decrease of 1-2 jiao to 3-4 jiao compared to the previous price. It is said that only 70-80 dan were offered in the market yesterday, which shows the decline of the market.

Hot-Rolled Steel: The market is weak due to the large supply, but practical can factories have stopped operations due to declining business, and sales have greatly declined. The market sentiment is also relatively soft. Old steel mills are estimated at 29 yuan, new steel mills at 18 yuan, unlicensed goods at 27 yuan, and Japanese goods at 16.75 yuan. It is said that only 100-200 boxes were traded in the market yesterday.

Bamboo Joint Silk: The market is overstocked. There is not much demand from the construction industry, and there are few customers buying. Recently, foreign firms have been selling their spot goods and stockpiled goods at the same time, dragging down the standards. The current market price is estimated at 97-98 yuan, while the single best style sells for only 94-95 yuan.
